\title{dung\_beetle\_landscape}
\author{Chloe Cho}
\date{2026-04-08}

\begin{document}
\maketitle

Read in data frame - landscape data pulled from USDA CDL at 1000m radius
around each trapping point. Convert data types.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{dung\_beetle }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{read.delim}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Data/diversity\_landscape.csv"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{sep =} \StringTok{","}\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{dung\_beetle }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ dung\_beetle }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{date =} \FunctionTok{as.Date}\NormalTok{(date, }\AttributeTok{format =} \StringTok{"\%m/\%d"}\NormalTok{)) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{farm =} \FunctionTok{as.factor}\NormalTok{(farm))}
  
\NormalTok{dung\_beetle}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{julian\_date }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{format}\NormalTok{(dung\_beetle}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{date, }\StringTok{"\%j"}\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{dung\_beetle }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ dung\_beetle }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{julian\_date =} \FunctionTok{as.numeric}\NormalTok{(julian\_date))}

\NormalTok{dung\_beetle}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{numeric\_date }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{as.numeric}\NormalTok{(dung\_beetle}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{date) }

\NormalTok{dung\_beetle}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\section{Total abundance}\label{total-abundance}

All models include year, Julian date, woodland proportion (forests,
shrublands), agriculture proportion (all agriculture types), and
semi-natural habitat proportion as fixed effects and farm as a random
effect.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]

\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}
